\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-configuration}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-configuration}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10463}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Configuration}{Configuration}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10463}

\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Set {\ttfamily parser} property to {\ttfamily @babel/eslint-\/parser}.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Add {\ttfamily plugins} section and specify {\ttfamily eslint-\/plugin-\/flowtype} as a plugin.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Enable rules.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-configuration-shareable-configurations}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-configuration-shareable-configurations}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10464}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Shareable configurations}{Shareable configurations}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10464}
\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-configuration-shareable-configurations-recommended}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-configuration-shareable-configurations-recommended}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10465}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Recommended}{Recommended}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10465}
This plugin exports a \href{./src/configs/recommended.json}{\texttt{ recommended configuration}} that enforces Flow type good practices.

To enable this configuration use the extends property in your {\ttfamily .eslintrc} config file\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}extends"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}plugin:flowtype/recommended"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ],}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}plugins"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


See \href{http://eslint.org/docs/user-guide/configuring\#extending-configuration-files}{\texttt{ ESLint documentation}} for more information about extending configuration files.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-settings-onlyfileswithflowannotation}%

 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10468}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$only\+Files\+With\+Flow\+Annotation$<$/code$>$}{<code>onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10468}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10469}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Rules}{Rules}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10469}
\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-array-style-complex-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-array-style-complex-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10470}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$array-\/style-\/complex-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>array-style-complex-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10470}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces a particular annotation style of complex types.

Type is considered complex in these cases\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/maybe/}{\texttt{ Maybe type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/functions/}{\texttt{ Function type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/objects/}{\texttt{ Object type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/tuples/}{\texttt{ Tuple type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/unions/}{\texttt{ Union type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/intersections/}{\texttt{ Intersection type}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

This rule takes one argument.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}verbose'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using}Type\mbox{[}\mbox{]}{\ttfamily instead of}Array$<$\+Type$>$\`{}.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}shorthand'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using}Array$<$\+Type$>${\ttfamily instead of}Type\mbox{[}\mbox{]}\`{}.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}verbose'\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (?string)[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<?string>"{},\ not\ "{}(?string)[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}verbose"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (?string)[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<?string>"{},\ not\ "{}(?string)[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}shorthand"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<?string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}(?string)[]"{},\ not\ "{}Array<?string>"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}shorthand"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<\{foo:\ string\}>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}\{foo:\ string\}[]"{},\ not\ "{}Array<\{foo:\ string\}>"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (string\ |\ number)[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<string\ |\ number>"{},\ not\ "{}(string\ |\ number)[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (string\ \&\ number)[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<string\ \&\ number>"{},\ not\ "{}(string\ \&\ number)[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ [string,\ number][]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<[string,\ number]>"{},\ not\ "{}[string,\ number][]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{foo:\ string\}[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<\{foo:\ string\}>"{},\ not\ "{}\{foo:\ string\}[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (string\ =>\ number)[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<string\ =>\ number>"{},\ not\ "{}(string\ =>\ number)[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ foo:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ bar:\ number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<\{\ foo:\ string,\ bar:\ number\ \}>"{},\ not\ "{}\{\ foo:\ string,\ bar:\ number\ \}[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ foo:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ bar:\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ quo:\ boolean,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ hey:\ Date}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<Type>"{},\ not\ "{}Type[]"{}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<?string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}verbose"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<?string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}shorthand"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (?string)[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}shorthand"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}shorthand"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<?string>}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-array-style-simple-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-array-style-simple-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10471}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$array-\/style-\/simple-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>array-style-simple-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10471}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces a particular array type annotation style of simple types.

Type is considered simple in these cases\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/primitives/}{\texttt{ Primitive types}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/literals/}{\texttt{ Literal types}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/mixed/}{\texttt{ Mixed type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/any/}{\texttt{ Any type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/classes/}{\texttt{ Class type}}
\item \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/generics/}{\texttt{ Generic type}}
\item Array type \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/arrays/\#toc-array-type-shorthand-syntax}{\texttt{ shorthand notation}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

This rule takes one argument.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}verbose'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using}Type\mbox{[}\mbox{]}{\ttfamily instead of}Array$<$\+Type$>$\`{}.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}shorthand'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using}Array$<$\+Type$>${\ttfamily instead of}Type\mbox{[}\mbox{]}\`{}.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}verbose'\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<string>"{},\ not\ "{}string[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}verbose"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<string>"{},\ not\ "{}string[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}shorthand"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}string[]"{},\ not\ "{}Array<string>"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Date[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<Date>"{},\ not\ "{}Date[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<string>[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<Promise<string>>"{},\ not\ "{}Promise<string>[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \$Keys<\{foo:\ string\}>[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<\$Keys<\{foo:\ string\}>>"{},\ not\ "{}\$Keys<\{foo:\ string\}>[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ any[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<any>"{},\ not\ "{}any[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ mixed[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<mixed>"{},\ not\ "{}mixed[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ void[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<void>"{},\ not\ "{}void[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ null[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<null>"{},\ not\ "{}null[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ foo:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ bar:\ number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}>[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<Promise<\{\ foo:\ string,\ bar:\ number\ \}>>"{},\ not\ "{}Promise<\{\ foo:\ string,\ bar:\ number\ \}>[]"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ foo:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ bar:\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ quo:\ boolean}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}>[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}Array<Type>"{},\ not\ "{}Type[]"{}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}verbose"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}shorthand"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<Array<string>>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}verbose"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (?string)[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}verbose"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ typeof\ Array}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-arrow-parens}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-arrow-parens}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10472}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$arrow-\/parens$<$/code$>$}{<code>arrow-parens</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10472}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces the consistent use of parentheses in arrow functions.

This rule has a string option and an object one.

String options are\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}} (default) requires parens around arguments in all cases.
\item {\ttfamily "{}as-\/needed"{}} enforces no braces where they can be omitted.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Object properties for variants of the {\ttfamily "{}as-\/needed"{}} option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}require\+For\+Block\+Body"{}\+: true} modifies the as-\/needed rule in order to require parens if the function body is in an instructions block (surrounded by braces).
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then(foo\ =>\ \{\});}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then(foo\ =>\ a);}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a(foo\ =>\ \{\ if\ (true)\ \{\};\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a(async\ foo\ =>\ \{\ if\ (true)\ \{\};\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a,)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async\ (a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async(a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async\ a\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async\ (a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async(a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ undefined}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{()\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then((foo)\ =>\ \{\});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then((foo)\ =>\ \{\ if\ (true)\ \{\};\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then(async\ (foo)\ =>\ \{\ if\ (true)\ \{\};\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{()\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a)\ =>\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then((foo)\ =>\ \{\});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then((foo)\ =>\ \{\ if\ (true)\ \{\};\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a.then(async\ (foo)\ =>\ \{\ if\ (true)\ \{\};\ \});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{()\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{([a,\ b])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{\ a,\ b\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{(a\ =\ 10)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(...a)\ =>\ a[0]}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a,\ b)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async\ ([a,\ b])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async\ (a,\ b)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a:\ T)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a):\ T\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{()\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{([a,\ b])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{(\{\ a,\ b\ \})\ =>\ a\ +\ b}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a\ =\ 10)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(...a)\ =>\ a[0]}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a,\ b)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{a\ =>\ (\{\})}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{async\ a\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}as-\/needed"{},\{"{}requireForBlockBody"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(a:\ T)\ =>\ a}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-boolean-style}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-boolean-style}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10473}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$boolean-\/style$<$/code$>$}{<code>boolean-style</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10473}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces a particular style for boolean type annotations. This rule takes one argument.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}boolean'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using}bool{\ttfamily instead of}boolean\`{}.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}bool'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using}boolean{\ttfamily instead of}bool\`{}.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}boolean'\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ bool}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}boolean"{},\ not\ "{}bool"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}boolean"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ bool}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}boolean"{},\ not\ "{}bool"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}bool"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ boolean}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}bool"{},\ not\ "{}boolean"{}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ boolean}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}boolean"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ boolean}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}bool"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ bool}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}boolean"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ bool}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-define-flow-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-define-flow-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10474}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$define-\/flow-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>define-flow-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10474}
Marks Flow type identifiers as defined.

Used to suppress \href{http://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-undef}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily no-\/undef}}} reporting of type identifiers.

The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ a:\ AType}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ a:\ AType;\ var\ b:\ AType}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ a;\ (a:\ AType)}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ a:\ AType<BType>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ A\ =\ AType}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ type\ A\ =\ number}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{opaque\ type\ A\ =\ AType}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ f(a:\ AType)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ f(a:\ AType.a)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ f(a:\ AType.a.b)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ f(a):\ AType\ \{\};\ var\ a:\ AType}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ f(a):\ AType\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ C\ \{\ a:\ AType\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ C\ \{\ a:\ AType.a\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ C\ \{\ a:\ AType.a.b\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ C\ implements\ AType\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ interface\ A\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{\ a:\ (\{b()\ \{\}\}:\ AType)\ \})}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{Y<AType>():\ BType\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/undef"{}:2\}}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-delimiter-dangle}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-delimiter-dangle}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10475}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$delimiter-\/dangle$<$/code$>$}{<code>delimiter-dangle</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10475}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent use of trailing commas in Object and Tuple annotations.

This rule takes three arguments where the possible values are the same as ESLint\textquotesingle{}s default {\ttfamily comma-\/dangle} rule\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item The first argument is for Object and Tuple annotations. The default value is `\textquotesingle{}never'{\ttfamily .}
\item {\ttfamily The second argument is used for Interface annotations. This defaults to the value of the first argument.}
\item {\ttfamily The third argument is used for inexact object notation (trailing}...{\ttfamily ). The default value is}\textquotesingle{}never\textquotesingle{}\`{}.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

If it is `\textquotesingle{}never'\`{} then a problem is raised when there is a trailing comma.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}always'\`{} then a problem is raised when there is no trailing comma.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}always-\/multiline'\`{} then a problem is raised when there is no trailing comma on a multi-\/line definition, or there {\itshape is} a trailing comma on a single-\/line definition.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}only-\/multiline'\`{} then a problem is raised when there is a trailing comma on a single-\/line definition. It allows, but does not enforce, trailing commas on multi-\/line definitions.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}

\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always-\/multiline"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always-\/multiline"{}]}

\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ string}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{},"{}never"{},"{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{[key:\ string]:\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{...;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\DoxyCodeLine{[key:\ string]:\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{...}

\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{},"{}never"{},"{}always-\/multiline"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{[key:\ string]:\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ [string,\ number,]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ [string,\ number,]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{number}
\DoxyCodeLine{]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ [string,\ number,]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{]}

\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}only-\/multiline"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ [\ number,\ string,\ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ trailing\ delimiter}

\end{DoxyCode}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-enforce-line-break}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-enforce-line-break}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10476}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$enforce-\/line-\/break$<$/code$>$}{<code>enforce-line-break</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10476}
This rule enforces line breaks between type definitions.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ baz\ =\ 6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ hi\ =\ 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ below\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ hi\ =\ 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ above\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ som\ =\ "{}jes"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ a\ comment}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ fed\ =\ "{}hed"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ above\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ som\ =\ "{}jes"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ a\ comment}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ fed\ =\ "{}hed"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ below\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ hello\ =\ 34;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ som\ =\ "{}jes"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ fed\ =\ "{}hed"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ below\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ above\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ a\ =\ 5;}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ hello\ =\ 34;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ above\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ a\ =\ 5;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ a\ comment}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ hello\ =\ 34;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ above\ type\ declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ a\ =\ 5;}
\DoxyCodeLine{/**}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ *\ a\ jsdoc\ block}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ */}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ hello\ =\ 34;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ New\ line\ required\ above\ type\ declaration}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ gjs\ =\ 6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ gjs\ =\ 6;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ hi\ =\ 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ red\ =\ "{}serpent"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{console.log("{}hello"{});}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ number\ or\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Y\ =\ string\ |\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ resting\ +\ sleep}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ snooze\ =\ "{}dreaming"{}\ |\ "{}"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ accountBalance:\ string\ |\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ accountNumber:\ string\ |\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ x\ =\ 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ y\ =\ 489;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Some\ Comment}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ accountBalance:\ string\ |\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ accountNumber:\ string\ |\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ RoadT\ =\ "{}grass"{}\ |\ "{}gravel"{}\ |\ "{}cement"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ A\ =\ string}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-generic-spacing}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-generic-spacing}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10477}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$generic-\/spacing$<$/code$>$}{<code>generic-spacing</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10477}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent spacing within generic type annotation parameters.

This rule takes one argument. If it is `\textquotesingle{}never'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when there is a space surrounding the generic type parameters. If it is}\textquotesingle{}always\textquotesingle{}\`{} then a problem is raised when there is no space surrounding the generic type parameters.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}never'\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ \ string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ FooBar<string\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}FooBar"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ string\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ (foo),\ bar,\ (((baz)))\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<string\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ FooBar<\ string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}FooBar"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<(foo),\ bar,\ (((baz)))>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ FooBar<\ \ string\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ one\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}FooBar"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ FooBar<\ string\ \ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ one\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}FooBar"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ \ (foo),\ bar,\ (((baz)))\ \ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ one\ space\ at\ start\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ one\ space\ at\ end\ of\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<(string)>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<(foo),\ bar,\ (((baz)))>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ (foo),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ bar,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ (((baz)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \ Promise<}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ (foo),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ bar,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ (((baz)))}
\DoxyCodeLine{>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ string\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ (string)\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<\ (foo),\ bar,\ (((baz)))\ >}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-interface-id-match}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-interface-id-match}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10478}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$interface-\/id-\/match$<$/code$>$}{<code>interface-id-match</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10478}
Enforces a consistent naming pattern for interfaces.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-interface-id-match-options}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-interface-id-match-options}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10479}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10479}
This rule requires a text Reg\+Exp\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/interface-\/id-\/match"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}\string^([A-\/Z][a-\/z0-\/9]*)+Type\$"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


`'\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}(\mbox{[}A-\/Z\mbox{]}\mbox{[}a-\/z0-\/9\mbox{]}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})+Type\$\$\textquotesingle{}\`{} is the default pattern.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ foo\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Interface\ identifier\ 'foo'\ does\ not\ match\ pattern\ '/\string^([A-\/Z][a-\/z0-\/9]*)+Type\$/u'.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}\string^foo\$"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ FooType\{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Interface\ identifier\ 'FooType'\ does\ not\ match\ pattern\ '/\string^foo\$/u'.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ FooType\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}\string^foo\$"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ foo\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ foo\ \{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-newline-after-flow-annotation}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-newline-after-flow-annotation}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10480}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$newline-\/after-\/flow-\/annotation$<$/code$>$}{<code>newline-after-flow-annotation</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10480}
This rule requires an empty line after the Flow annotation.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-newline-after-flow-annotation-options-1}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-newline-after-flow-annotation-options-1}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10481}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10481}
The rule has a string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}} (default)\+: Enforces that {\ttfamily @flow} annotations be followed by an empty line, separated by newline (LF)
\item {\ttfamily "{}always-\/windows"{}}\+: Identical to "{}always"{}, but will use a CRLF when autofixing
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}}\+: Enforces that {\ttfamily @flow} annotations are not followed by empty lines
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/newline-\/after-\/flow-\/annotation"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ Foo\ from\ './foo';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ newline\ after\ flow\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ Foo\ from\ './foo';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ newline\ after\ flow\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always-\/windows"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ Foo\ from\ './foo';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ newline\ after\ flow\ annotation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ no\ newline\ after\ flow\ annotation}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ Foo\ from\ './foo';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always-\/windows"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ Foo\ from\ './foo';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ Foo\ from\ './foo';}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-dupe-keys}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-dupe-keys}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10482}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$no-\/dupe-\/keys$<$/code$>$}{<code>no-dupe-keys</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10482}
Checks for duplicate properties in Object annotations.

This rule mirrors ESLint\textquotesingle{}s \href{http://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-dupe-keys}{\texttt{ no-\/dupe-\/keys}} rule.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/no-\/dupe-\/keys"{}:\ 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ b:\ string,\ a:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ b:\ string,\ a:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ "{}a"{}):\ string,\ get(key:\ "{}a"{}):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ 1):\ string,\ get(key:\ 1):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ 1.1):\ string,\ get(key:\ 1.1):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ true):\ string,\ get(key:\ true):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ \{a:\ 1\}):\ string,\ get(key:\ \{a:\ 1\}):string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ a\ =\ "{}a"{};\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ a):\ string,\ get(key:\ a):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ b\ =\ 1;\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ b):\ string,\ get(key:\ b):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ c\ =\ true;\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ c):\ string,\ get(key:\ c):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ d\ =\ \{\};\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ d):\ string,\ get(key:\ d):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ e\ =\ [];\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ e):\ string,\ get(key:\ e):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ e\ =\ [1,\ "{}a"{}];\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ e):\ string,\ get(key:\ e):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ fn()\ \{\};\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ fn):\ string,\ get(key:\ fn):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ property.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ b:\ string,\ c:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ b:\ string,\ a:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ "{}a"{}):\ string,\ get(key:\ "{}b"{}):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ 1):\ string,\ get(key:\ 2):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ 1.1):\ string,\ get(key:\ 1.2):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ true):\ string,\ get(key:\ false):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ ["{}a"{},\ 1]):\ string,\ get(key:\ ["{}a"{},\ 2]):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ ["{}a"{},\ ["{}b"{},\ 1]]):\ string,\ get(key:\ ["{}a"{},\ ["{}b"{},\ 2]]):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ b:\ string,\ c:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ "{}a"{}):\ string,\ get(key:\ "{}b"{}):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ "{}a"{}):\ string,\ get(key:\ "{}a"{},\ key2:\ "{}b"{}):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ "{}a"{}):\ string,\ get(key:\ 1):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ \{\ a:\ 1\ \}):\ string,\ get(key:\ \{\ a:\ 2\ \}):\ string\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ a\ =\ \{\};\ var\ b\ =\ \{\};\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ a):\ string,\ get(key:\ b):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ a\ =\ 1;\ var\ b\ =\ 1;\ type\ f\ =\ \{\ get(key:\ a):\ string,\ get(key:\ b):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ a\ =\ \{\ b:\ <C>(config:\ \{\ ...C,\ key:\ string\})\ =>\ C\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ interface\ Foo\ \{\ get\ foo():\ boolean;\ get\ bar():\ string;\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-duplicate-type-union-intersection-members}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-duplicate-type-union-intersection-members}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10483}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$no-\/duplicate-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members$<$/code$>$}{<code>no-duplicate-type-union-intersection-members</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10483}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Checks for duplicate members of a type union/intersection.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-duplicate-type-union-intersection-members-options-2}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-duplicate-type-union-intersection-members-options-2}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10484}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10484}
You can disable checking intersection types using {\ttfamily check\+Intersections}.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true} (default) -\/ check for duplicate members of intersection members.
\item {\ttfamily false} -\/ do not check for duplicate members of intersection members.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/no-\/duplicate-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}checkIntersections"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can disable checking union types using {\ttfamily check\+Unions}.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true} (default) -\/ check for duplicate members of union members.
\item {\ttfamily false} -\/ do not check for duplicate members of union members.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/no-\/duplicate-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}checkUnions"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ A\ =\ 1\ |\ 2\ |\ 3\ |\ 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ union\ member\ found\ "{}1"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ B\ =\ 'foo'\ |\ 'bar'\ |\ 'foo';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ union\ member\ found\ "{}'foo'"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ C\ =\ A\ |\ B\ |\ A\ |\ B;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ union\ member\ found\ "{}A"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ union\ member\ found\ "{}B"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ C\ =\ A\ \&\ B\ \&\ A\ \&\ B;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ intersection\ member\ found\ "{}A"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Duplicate\ intersection\ member\ found\ "{}B"{}.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ A\ =\ 1\ |\ 2\ |\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ B\ =\ 'foo'\ |\ 'bar';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ C\ =\ A\ |\ B;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ C\ =\ A\ \&\ B;}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-existential-type}%

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-flow-fix-me-comments}%

This is especially useful as a warning to ensure instances of {\ttfamily \$Flow\+Fix\+Me} in your codebase get fixed over time.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-mutable-array}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-mutable-array}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10490}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$no-\/mutable-\/array$<$/code$>$}{<code>no-mutable-array</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10490}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Requires use of \href{https://github.com/facebook/flow/blob/v0.46.0/lib/core.js\#L185}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily \$Read\+Only\+Array}}} instead of just {\ttfamily Array} or array \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/arrays/\#toc-array-type-shorthand-syntax}{\texttt{ shorthand notation}}. {\ttfamily \$Read\+Only\+Array} is immutable array collection type and the superclass of Array and tuple types in Flow. Use of {\ttfamily \$Read\+Only\+Array} instead of {\ttfamily Array} can solve some "{}problems"{} in typing with Flow (e.\+g., \href{https://github.com/facebook/flow/issues/3425}{\texttt{ 1}}, \href{https://github.com/facebook/flow/issues/4251}{\texttt{ 2}}).

General reasons for using immutable data structures\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item They are simpler to construct, test, and use
\item They help to avoid temporal coupling
\item Their usage is side-\/effect free (no defensive copies)
\item Identity mutability problem is avoided
\item They always have failure atomicity
\item They are much easier to cache
\end{DoxyItemize}

Note that initialization of a variable with an empty array is considered valid (e.\+g., {\ttfamily const values\+: Array\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}string\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} = \mbox{[}\mbox{]};}). This behavior resembles the behavior of Flow\textquotesingle{}s \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/objects/\#toc-unsealed-objects}{\texttt{ unsealed objects}}, as it is assumed that empty array is intended to be mutated.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Array<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}\$ReadOnlyArray"{}\ instead\ of\ "{}Array"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string[]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}\$ReadOnlyArray"{}\ instead\ of\ array\ shorthand\ notation}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ values:\ Array<Array<string>>\ =\ [];}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}\$ReadOnlyArray"{}\ instead\ of\ "{}Array"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{let\ values:\ Array<Array<string>>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}\$ReadOnlyArray"{}\ instead\ of\ "{}Array"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ "{}\$ReadOnlyArray"{}\ instead\ of\ "{}Array"{}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \$ReadOnlyArray<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ values:\ Array<\$ReadOnlyArray<string>>\ =\ [];}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ values:\ \$ReadOnlyArray<string>[]\ =\ [];}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ values:\ Array<\$ReadOnlyArray<string>>\ =\ new\ Array();}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ values:\ Array<\$ReadOnlyArray<string>>\ =\ Array();}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-primitive-constructor-types}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-primitive-constructor-types}%

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-types-missing-file-annotation}%

 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10492}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$no-\/types-\/missing-\/file-\/annotation$<$/code$>$}{<code>no-types-missing-file-annotation</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10492}
Disallows Flow type imports, aliases, and annotations in files missing a valid Flow file declaration (or a @noflow annotation).


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ an\ unrelated\ comment}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ \{A\}\ from\ "{}a"{}}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-unused-expressions}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-unused-expressions}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10493}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$no-\/unused-\/expressions$<$/code$>$}{<code>no-unused-expressions</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10493}
An extension of \href{https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unused-expressions}{\texttt{ ESLint\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily no-\/unused-\/expressions}}}. This rule ignores type cast expressions and optional call expressions, but otherwise behaves the same as ESLint\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily no-\/unused-\/expressions}.

Bare type casts are useful, for example to assert the exhaustiveness of a {\ttfamily switch}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Action}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ =\ \{\ type:\ 'FOO',\ doFoo:\ (\_:\ number)\ =>\ void\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ |\ \{\ type:\ 'BAR',\ doBar:\ (\_:\ string)\ =>\ void\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ State\ =\ \{\ foo:\ number,\ bar:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ runFooBar(action:\ Action,\ state:\ State):\ void\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ switch\ (action.type)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ case\ 'FOO':}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ doFoo(state.foo);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ break;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ case\ 'BAR':}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ doBar(state.bar);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ break;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ default:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ (action:\ empty);\ \ //\ type\ error\ when\ \`{}Action`\ is\ extended\ with\ new\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ console.error(`Impossible\ action:\ \$\{action.toString()\}`);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


This rule takes the same arguments as ESLint\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily no-\/unused-\/expressions}. See \href{https://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unused-expressions}{\texttt{ that rule\textquotesingle{}s documentation}} for details.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{foo\ +\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ an\ assignment\ or\ function\ call\ and\ instead\ saw\ an\ expression.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{x?.y}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ an\ assignment\ or\ function\ call\ and\ instead\ saw\ an\ expression.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ number)}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{x?.y()}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-weak-types}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-no-weak-types}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10494}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$no-\/weak-\/types$<$/code$>$}{<code>no-weak-types</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10494}
Warns against weak type annotations {\itshape any}, {\itshape Object} and {\itshape Function}. These types can cause flow to silently skip over portions of your code, which would have otherwise caused type errors.

This rule optionally takes one argument, an object to configure which type warnings to enable. By default, all of the warnings are enabled. e.\+g. to disable the {\ttfamily any} warning (allowing it to exist in your code), while continuing to warn about {\ttfamily Object} and {\ttfamily Function}\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/no-\/weak-\/types"{}:\ [2,\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}any"{}:\ false,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}Object"{}:\ true,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}Function"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ or,\ the\ following\ is\ equivalent\ as\ default\ is\ true:}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/no-\/weak-\/types"{}:\ [2,\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}any"{}:\ false}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ any\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Promise<any>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Promise<Promise<any>>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Object\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Promise<Object>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Promise<Promise<Object>>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Function\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Promise<Function>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Promise<Promise<Function>>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ any)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ Function)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo?:\ any)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo?:\ Function)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ \{\ a:\ any\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ \{\ a:\ Object\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ any[])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ any}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ Function}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ any\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ Object\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ (a:\ Object):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ (a:\ string):\ Function\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing:\ any)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing:\ Object)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo:\ Function}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo:\ Object}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ props:\ any\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ props:\ Object\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo:\ any}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}Function"{}:false\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ any;\ type\ Y\ =\ Function;\ type\ Z\ =\ Object}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}any"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Object"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}any"{}:false,"{}Object"{}:false\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ any;\ type\ Y\ =\ Function;\ type\ Z\ =\ Object}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ use\ of\ weak\ type\ "{}Function"{}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ string\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Promise<string>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ \{\ a:\ string\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ \{\ a:\ ?string\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ string[])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ (a:\ string):\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing:\ string)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}any"{}:false,"{}Object"{}:false\}]}

\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}Function"{}:false\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Function}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(thing):\ Function\ \{\}}
