\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-object-type-curly-spacing}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-object-type-curly-spacing}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10495}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$object-\/type-\/curly-\/spacing$<$/code$>$}{<code>object-type-curly-spacing</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10495}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

This rule enforces consistent spacing inside braces of object types.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-object-type-curly-spacing-options-4}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-object-type-curly-spacing-options-4}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10496}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10496}
The rule has a string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}} (default)\+: disallows spacing inside of braces.
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}}\+: requires spacing inside of braces.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ after\ "{}\{"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{},\ ...\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{|"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}\ |\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}|\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{},\ [key:\ string]:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{},\ [key:\ string]:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ baz:\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\},\ bar:\ 4\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ after\ "{}\{"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ after\ "{}\{"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ after\ "{}\{"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ baz:\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\},\ bar:\ 4\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ after\ "{}\{"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ baz:\ \{\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\ \},\ bar:\ 4\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{},\ ...\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ before\ "{}\}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{|"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}\ |\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ after\ "{}\{|"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{},\ [key:\ string]:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ A\ space\ is\ required\ after\ "{}\{"{}.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{baz:\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\},\ bar:\ 4\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{foo:\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{foo:\ "{}bar"{}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{foo:\ "{}bar"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ "{}bar"{}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ "{}bar"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ "{}bar"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{ee:\ "{}bar"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ "{}bar"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{ee:\ "{}bar"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{|"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}|\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{"{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{},\ [key:\ string]:\ string\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ baz:\ \{\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\ \},\ bar:\ 4\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{foo:\ "{}bar"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ baz:\ 4\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{|\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{}\ |\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}bar"{},\ [key:\ string]:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{\ \ baz:\ \{\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\ \},\ bar:\ 4\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ obj\ =\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ baz:\ \{\ "{}foo"{}:\ "{}qux"{}\ \},\ bar:\ 4}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-object-type-delimiter}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-object-type-delimiter}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10497}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$object-\/type-\/delimiter$<$/code$>$}{<code>object-type-delimiter</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10497}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent separators between properties in Flow object types.

This rule takes one argument.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}comma'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using};\`{} as a separator.

If it is `\textquotesingle{}semicolon'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when using},\`{} as a separator.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}comma'\`{}.

{\itshape This rule is ported from {\ttfamily babel/flow-\/object-\/type}, however the default option was changed.}

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ Foo,\ b:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ semicolons\ to\ commas\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ Foo;\ b:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ commas\ to\ semicolons\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo,\ [b:\ string]:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ semicolons\ to\ commas\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo;\ [b:\ string]:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ commas\ to\ semicolons\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ ():\ Foo,\ ():\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ semicolons\ to\ commas\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ ():\ Foo;\ ():\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ commas\ to\ semicolons\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ a:\ Foo,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ semicolons\ to\ commas\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ a:\ Foo;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ commas\ to\ semicolons\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ semicolons\ to\ commas\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ a:\ Foo;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ commas\ to\ semicolons\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ ():\ Foo,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ semicolons\ to\ commas\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ ():\ Foo;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ commas\ to\ semicolons\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ static\ ():\ Foo,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ semicolons\ to\ commas\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ static\ ():\ Foo;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Prefer\ commas\ to\ semicolons\ in\ object\ and\ class\ types}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ Foo;\ b:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ Foo,\ b:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo;\ [b:\ string]:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo,\ [b:\ string]:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ ():\ Foo;\ ():\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ ():\ Foo,\ ():\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ Foo,\ b:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo,\ [b:\ string]:\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ ():\ Foo,\ ():\ Bar\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ a:\ Foo;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ a:\ Foo,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ [a:\ string]:\ Foo,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ ():\ Foo;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}comma"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ ():\ Foo,\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}semicolon"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ a:\ Foo,\ b:\ Bar\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-quotes}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-quotes}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10498}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$quotes$<$/code$>$}{<code>quotes</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10498}
Enforces single quotes or double quotes around string literals.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-quotes-options-5}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-quotes-options-5}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10499}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10499}
The rule has string options of\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}double"{}} (default) requires double quotes around string literals.
\item {\ttfamily "{}single"{}} requires single quotes around string literals.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ 'hi'}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ double\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}double"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ 'hello'\ |\ 'test'\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ double\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ double\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}double"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ "{}hello"{}\ |\ 'test',\ t:\ 'hello'\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ double\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ double\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}single"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ "{}hi"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ single\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}single"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ "{}hello"{}\ |\ "{}test"{}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ single\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ single\ quote.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}single"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ "{}hello"{}\ |\ 'test',\ t:\ 'hello'\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ String\ literals\ must\ use\ single\ quote.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}double"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ "{}hi"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}double"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ "{}hello"{}\ |\ "{}test"{}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}double"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ "{}hello"{}\ |\ "{}test"{},\ t:\ "{}hello"{}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}single"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ 'hi'}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}single"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ 'hello'\ |\ 'test'\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}single"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T\ =\ \{\ test:\ 'hello'\ |\ 'test',\ t:\ 'hello'\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-compound-type-alias}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-compound-type-alias}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10500}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/compound-\/type-\/alias$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-compound-type-alias</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10500}
Requires to make a type alias for all \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/unions/}{\texttt{ union}} and \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/intersections/}{\texttt{ intersection}} types. If these are used in "{}raw"{} forms it might be tempting to just copy \& paste them around the code. However, this brings sort of a source code pollution and unnecessary changes on several parts when these compound types need to be changed.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-compound-type-alias-options-6}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-compound-type-alias-options-6}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10501}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10501}
The rule has two options\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item a string option
\end{DoxyEnumerate}
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}} (default)
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item an object
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/compound-\/type-\/alias"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}allowNull"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}



\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily allow\+Null} allows compound types where one of the members is a {\ttfamily null}, e.\+g. {\ttfamily string \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} null}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{},\{"{}allowNull"{}:false\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo:\ string\ |\ null\ =\ null;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ union\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(bar:\ "{}A"{}\ |\ "{}B"{})\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ union\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo:\ "{}A"{}\ |\ "{}B"{}\ =\ "{}A"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ union\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ "{}A"{}\ |\ "{}B"{}\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ union\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(bar:\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ |\ \{\ s:\ string\ \})\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ union\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(bar:\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ \&\ \{\ s:\ string\ \})\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ intersection\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo:\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ \&\ \{\ s:\ string\ \}\ =\ \{\ n:\ 0,\ s:\ "{}"{}\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ intersection\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ \&\ \{\ s:\ string\ \}\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ intersection\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(bar:\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ \&\ \{\ s:\ string\ \})\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ intersection\ types\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ named\ type\ alias.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo:\ string\ |\ null\ =\ null;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{},\{"{}allowNull"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo:\ string\ |\ null\ =\ null;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ "{}A"{}\ |\ "{}B"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Bar\ =\ "{}A"{}\ |\ "{}B"{};\ function\ foo(bar:\ Bar)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ disjoint:\ "{}A"{},\ n:\ number\ \}\ |\ \{\ disjoint:\ "{}B"{},\ s:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ \&\ \{\ s:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Bar\ =\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ \&\ \{\ s:\ string\ \};\ function\ foo(bar:\ Bar)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(bar:\ "{}A"{}\ |\ "{}B"{})\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ foo(bar:\ \{\ n:\ number\ \}\ \&\ \{\ s:\ string\ \})\ \{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-exact-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-exact-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10502}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/exact-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-exact-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10502}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

This rule enforces \href{https://flow.org/en/docs/types/objects/\#toc-exact-object-types}{\texttt{ exact object types}}.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-exact-type-options-7}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-exact-type-options-7}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10503}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10503}
The rule has one string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}} (default)\+: Report all object type definitions that aren\textquotesingle{}t exact.
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}}\+: Report all object type definitions that are exact.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/exact-\/type"{}:\ [}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/exact-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}never"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ Array<\{bar:\ string\}>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ Array<\{bar:\ string\}>)\ =>\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ StackFrame\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ colno?:\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ lineno?:\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ filename?:\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ function?:\ \{\ name:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ not\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ bar:\ string\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ not\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ \{|\ baz:\ string\ |\}\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ not\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ Array<\{|\ bar:\ string\ |\}>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ not\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ Array<\{|\ bar:\ string\ |\}>)\ =>\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ not\ be\ exact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ StackFrame\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ colno?:\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ lineno?:\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ filename?:\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ function?:\ \{|\ name:\ string\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Object\ type\ must\ not\ be\ exact.}

\end{DoxyCode}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-indexer-name}%

 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10504}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/indexer-\/name$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-indexer-name</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10504}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

This rule validates Flow object indexer name.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-indexer-name-options-8}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-indexer-name-options-8}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10505}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10505}
The rule has a string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}} (default)\+: Never report files that are missing an indexer key name.
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}}\+: Always report files that are missing an indexer key name.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/indexer-\/name"{}:\ [}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ [string]:\ number\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ indexers\ must\ be\ declared\ with\ key\ name.}

\end{DoxyCode}

\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ [string]:\ number\ \};}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-inexact-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-inexact-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10506}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/inexact-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-inexact-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10506}
This rule enforces explicit inexact object types.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-inexact-type-options-9}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-inexact-type-options-9}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10507}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10507}
The rule has one string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}} (default)\+: Report all object type definitions that aren\textquotesingle{}t explicit inexact, but ignore exact objects.
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}}\+: Report all object type definitions that are explicit inexact.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/inexact-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/inexact-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}never"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ must\ be\ explicit\ inexact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ must\ be\ explicit\ inexact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ must\ be\ explicit\ inexact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ must\ be\ explicit\ inexact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{...\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ must\ not\ be\ explicit\ inexact.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ string,\ ...\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ must\ not\ be\ explicit\ inexact.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string,\ ...\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{interface\ Foo\ \{\ foo:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ Foo\ \{\ foo:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ bar:\ string\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ [key:\ string]:\ string,\ ...\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{...\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ string,\ ...\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ bar:\ string\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\ bar:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{|\ bar:\ string\ |\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ number;}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-parameter-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-parameter-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10508}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/parameter-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-parameter-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10508}
Requires that all function parameters have type annotations.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-parameter-type-options-10}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-parameter-type-options-10}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10509}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10509}
You can skip all arrow functions by providing the {\ttfamily exclude\+Arrow\+Functions} option with {\ttfamily true}.

Alternatively, you can want to exclude only concise arrow functions (e.\+g. {\ttfamily x =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} x \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} 2}). Provide {\ttfamily exclude\+Arrow\+Functions} with {\ttfamily expressions\+Only} for this.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/parameter-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/parameter-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:\ "{}expressionsOnly"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can exclude parameters that match a certain regex by using {\ttfamily exclude\+Parameter\+Match}.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/parameter-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}excludeParameterMatch"{}:\ "{}\string^\_"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


This excludes all parameters that start with an underscore ({\ttfamily \+\_\+}). The default pattern is {\ttfamily a\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}}, which doesn\textquotesingle{}t match anything, i.\+e., all parameters are checked.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x(foo)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x(foo)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo\ =\ 'FOO')\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(...foo)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{foo\})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}\{foo\}"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{([foo])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}[foo]"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{foo\ =\ 1\}\ =\ \{\})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}\{foo\ =\ 1\}"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ @flow}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:"{}expressionsOnly"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:"{}expressionsOnly"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x(foo)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeParameterMatch"{}:"{}\string^\_"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\_foo:\ number,\ bar)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}bar"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeParameterMatch"{}:"{}\string^\_"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\_foo,\ bar)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}bar"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ string\ =\ 'FOO')\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(...foo:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ f:\ Foo\ =\ (a,\ b)\ =>\ 42;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{foo\}:\ \{foo:\ string\})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{([foo]:\ Array)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ fn\ =\ (a:\ string,\ b:\ number)\ =>\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ f:\ fn\ =\ (a,\ b)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:"{}expressionsOnly"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo)\ =>\ 3}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeParameterMatch"{}:"{}\string^\_"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\_foo,\ bar:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeParameterMatch"{}:"{}\string^\_"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\_foo:\ number,\ bar:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo)\ =>\ \{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-readonly-react-props}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-readonly-react-props}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10510}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/readonly-\/react-\/props$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-readonly-react-props</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10510}
This rule validates that React props are marked as {\ttfamily \$Read\+Only}. React props are immutable and modifying them could lead to unexpected results. Marking prop shapes as {\ttfamily \$Read\+Only} avoids these issues.

The rule tries its best to work with both class and functional components. For class components, it does a fuzzy check for one of "{}\+Component"{}, "{}\+Pure\+Component"{}, "{}\+React.\+Component"{} and "{}\+React.\+Pure\+Component"{}. It doesn\textquotesingle{}t actually infer that those identifiers resolve to a proper {\ttfamily React.\+Component} object.

For example, this will NOT be checked\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ MyReact\ from\ 'react';}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ MyReact.Component\ \{\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


As a result, you can safely use other classes without getting warnings from this rule\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ MyClass\ extends\ MySuperClass\ \{\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


React\textquotesingle{}s functional components are hard to detect statically. The way it\textquotesingle{}s done here is by searching for JSX within a function. When present, a function is considered a React component\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ this\ gets\ checked}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ MyComponent(props:\ Props)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ return\ <p\ />;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ this\ doesn't\ get\ checked\ since\ no\ JSX\ is\ present\ in\ a\ function}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Options\ =\ \{\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ SomeHelper(options:\ Options)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ //\ ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ this\ doesn't\ get\ checked\ since\ no\ JSX\ is\ present\ directly\ in\ a\ function}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ helper()\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ MyComponent(props:\ Props)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ return\ helper();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The rule only works for locally defined props that are marked with a {\ttfamily \$Read\+Only} or using covariant notation. It doesn\textquotesingle{}t work with imported props\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ the\ rule\ has\ no\ way\ of\ knowing\ whether\ ImportedProps\ are\ read-\/only}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ type\ ImportedProps\ \}\ from\ './somewhere';}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<ImportedProps>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ the\ rule\ also\ checks\ for\ covariant\ properties}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ +foo:\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Bar\ extends\ React.Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ this\ fails\ because\ the\ object\ is\ not\ fully\ read-\/only}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ +foo:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ bar:\ number,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Bar\ extends\ React.Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ this\ fails\ because\ spreading\ makes\ object\ mutable\ (as\ of\ Flow\ 0.98)}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ https://github.com/gajus/eslint-\/plugin-\/flowtype/pull/400\#issuecomment-\/489813899}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ +foo:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ...bar,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Bar\ extends\ React.Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}



\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/readonly-\/react-\/props"{}:\ 2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


Optionally, you can enable support for \href{https://medium.com/flow-type/on-the-roadmap-exact-objects-by-default-16b72933c5cf}{\texttt{ implicit exact Flow types}} (useful when using {\ttfamily exact\+\_\+by\+\_\+default=true} Flow option)\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/readonly-\/react-\/props"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ \};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ OtherProps\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string\ \};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<OtherProps>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ OtherProps\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<\{\}>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Foo\ class\ props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ bar:\ \{\}\ \};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<Props,\ State>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ \};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ \};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ PureComponent<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ Props\ =\ \{\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|\ foo:\ string\ |\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|\ foo:\ string\ |\}\ |\ \{|\ bar:\ number\ |\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ foo:\ string\ \}\ |\ \{\ bar:\ number\ \};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|\ +foo:\ string,\ ...bar\ |\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|\ +foo:\ string,\ -\/bar:\ number\ |\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ \};\ function\ Foo(props:\ Props)\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ \};\ function\ Foo(props:\ Props)\ \{\ return\ foo\ ?\ <p\ />\ :\ <span\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ Foo(props:\ \{\})\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Foo\ component\ props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ Props\ =\ \{\};\ function\ Foo(props:\ Props)\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Props\ must\ be\ \$ReadOnly}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<\$ReadOnly<\{\}>>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ class\ Foo\ extends\ React.PureComponent<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<\$ReadOnly<\{\},\ State>>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<Props,\ State>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ class\ Foo\ extends\ PureComponent<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Bar<FooType>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props,\ State>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ export\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|\ +foo:\ string\ |\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|\ +foo:\ string,\ +bar:\ number\ |\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{|\ +foo:\ string\ |\}\ |\ \{|\ +bar:\ number\ |\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\ +foo:\ string\ \}\ |\ \{\ +bar:\ number\ \};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \$FlowFixMe;\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{||\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{||\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<\{||\}>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<\{||\}>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ Component<\{\}>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<UnknownProps>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{\ type\ Props\ \}\ from\ "{}file"{};\ class\ Foo\ extends\ React.Component<Props>\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\};\ function\ Foo()\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{\}>;\ function\ Foo(props:\ Props)\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Props\ =\ \{\};\ function\ Foo(props:\ OtherProps)\ \{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ Foo()\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ Foo(props:\ \$FlowFixMe)\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ Foo(props:\ \{||\})\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ Foo(props:\ \{||\})\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}useImplicitExactTypes"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ Foo(props:\ \{\})\ \{\ return\ <p\ />\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-return-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-return-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10511}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/return-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-return-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10511}
Requires that functions have return type annotation.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-return-type-options-11}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-return-type-options-11}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10512}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10512}
You can skip all arrow functions by providing the {\ttfamily exclude\+Arrow\+Functions} option with {\ttfamily true}.

Alternatively, you can exclude a concise arrow function (e.\+g. {\ttfamily () =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} 2}). Provide {\ttfamily exclude\+Arrow\+Functions} with {\ttfamily expressions\+Only} for this.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/return-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/return-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}excludeArrowFunctions"{}:\ "{}expressionsOnly"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can exclude or include specific tests with the {\ttfamily include\+Only\+Matching} and {\ttfamily exclude\+Matching} rules.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

Both rules take an array that can contain either strings or valid Reg\+Exp statements.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-types-at-top}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-types-at-top}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10513}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/types-\/at-\/top$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-types-at-top</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10513}
Requires all type declarations to be at the top of the file, after any import declarations.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-types-at-top-options-12}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-types-at-top-options-12}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10514}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10514}
The rule has a string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}}
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}}
\end{DoxyItemize}

The default value is {\ttfamily "{}always"{}}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ type\ declaration\ must\ be\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ file,\ after\ any\ import\ declarations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{opaque\ type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ type\ declaration\ must\ be\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ file,\ after\ any\ import\ declarations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ type\ declaration\ must\ be\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ file,\ after\ any\ import\ declarations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ opaque\ type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ type\ declaration\ must\ be\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ file,\ after\ any\ import\ declarations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number\ |\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ type\ declaration\ must\ be\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ file,\ after\ any\ import\ declarations.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ bar\ from\ "{}./bar"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ All\ type\ declaration\ must\ be\ at\ the\ top\ of\ the\ file,\ after\ any\ import\ declarations.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{opaque\ type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{export\ opaque\ type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ bar\ from\ "{}./bar"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ bar\ from\ "{}./bar"{};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ foo\ =\ 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ number;}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-valid-file-annotation}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-valid-file-annotation}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10515}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/valid-\/file-\/annotation$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-valid-file-annotation</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10515}
This rule validates Flow file annotations.

This rule can optionally report missing or missed placed annotations, common typos (e.\+g. {\ttfamily // @floww}), and enforce a consistent annotation style.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-valid-file-annotation-options-13}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-valid-file-annotation-options-13}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10516}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10516}
The rule has a string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}} (default)\+: Never report files that are missing an {\ttfamily @flow} annotation.
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}}\+: Always report files that are missing an {\ttfamily @flow} annotation
\end{DoxyItemize}

This rule has an object option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}annotation\+Style"{}} -\/ Enforce a consistent file annotation style.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}none"{}} (default)\+: Either annotation style is accepted.
\item {\ttfamily "{}line"{}}\+: Require single line annotations (i.\+e. {\ttfamily // @flow}).
\item {\ttfamily "{}block"{}}\+: Require block annotations (i.\+e. {\ttfamily /\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} @flow \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}/}).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}strict"{}} -\/ Enforce a strict flow file annotation.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily false} (default)\+: strict flow annotation is not required.
\item {\ttfamily true}\+: Require strict flow annotation (i.\+e. {\ttfamily // @flow strict}).
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/valid-\/file-\/annotation"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/valid-\/file-\/annotation"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}always"{},\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}annotationStyle"{}:\ "{}block"{},}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}strict"{}:\ true,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-variable-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-variable-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10517}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$require-\/variable-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>require-variable-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10517}
Requires that all variable declarators have type annotations.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-variable-type-options-14}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-require-variable-type-options-14}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10518}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10518}
You can exclude variables that match a certain regex by using {\ttfamily exclude\+Variable\+Match}.

This excludes all parameters that start with an underscore ({\ttfamily \+\_\+}). The default pattern is {\ttfamily a\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}}, which doesn\textquotesingle{}t match anything, i.\+e., all parameters are checked.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/variable-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}excludeVariableMatch"{}:\ "{}\string^\_"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can choose specific variable types ({\ttfamily var}, {\ttfamily let}, and {\ttfamily const}) to ignore using {\ttfamily exclude\+Variable\+Types}.

This excludes {\ttfamily var} and {\ttfamily let} declarations from needing type annotations, but forces {\ttfamily const} declarations to have it. By default, all declarations are checked.


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/require-\/variable-\/type"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}excludeVariableTypes"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}var"{}:\ true,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}let"{}:\ true,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}const"{}:\ false,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo\ =\ "{}bar"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}foo"{}\ variable\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo\ :\ string\ =\ "{}bar"{},\ bar\ =\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}bar"{}\ variable\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeVariableMatch"{}:"{}\string^\_"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ \_foo\ =\ "{}bar"{},\ bar\ =\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}bar"{}\ variable\ type\ annotation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeVariableTypes"{}:\{"{}let"{}:false,"{}var"{}:true\}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo\ =\ "{}bar"{},\ bar\ =\ 1;\ const\ oob\ :\ string\ =\ "{}oob"{};\ let\ hey\ =\ "{}yah"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ "{}hey"{}\ variable\ type\ annotation.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo\ :\ string\ =\ "{}bar"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo\ :\ string\ =\ "{}bar"{},\ bar\ :\ number\ =\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeVariableMatch"{}:"{}\string^\_"{}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ \_foo\ =\ "{}bar"{},\ bar\ :\ number\ =\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeVariableTypes"{}:\{"{}var"{}:true\}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo\ =\ "{}bar"{},\ bar\ =\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ [\{"{}excludeVariableTypes"{}:\{"{}let"{}:true,"{}var"{}:true\}\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ foo\ =\ "{}bar"{},\ bar\ =\ 1;\ const\ oob\ :\ string\ =\ "{}oob"{};\ let\ hey\ =\ "{}yah"{}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-semi}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-semi}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10519}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$semi$<$/code$>$}{<code>semi</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10519}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent use of semicolons after type aliases.

This rule takes one argument. If it is `\textquotesingle{}never'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when there is a semicolon after a type alias. If it is}\textquotesingle{}always\textquotesingle{}\`{} then a problem is raised when there is no semicolon after a type alias.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}always'\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ foo:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ semicolon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ foo:\ string;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Extra\ semicolon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ []}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ semicolon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ semicolon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Extra\ semicolon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ []}
\DoxyCodeLine{opaque\ type\ FooType\ =\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Missing\ semicolon.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ foo:\ string;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ foo:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ b:\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ b:\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{opaque\ type\ FooType\ =\ \{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-keys}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-keys}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10520}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$sort-\/keys$<$/code$>$}{<code>sort-keys</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10520}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces natural, case-\/insensitive sorting of Object annotations.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-keys-options-15}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-keys-options-15}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10521}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10521}
The first option specifies sort order.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}asc"{}} (default) -\/ enforce ascending sort order.
\item {\ttfamily "{}desc"{}} -\/ enforce descending sort order.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/sort-\/keys"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ "{}asc"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ c:\ number,\ b:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ type\ annotations\ to\ be\ in\ ascending\ order.\ "{}b"{}\ must\ be\ before\ "{}c"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}desc"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ b:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ type\ annotations\ to\ be\ in\ descending\ order.\ "{}b"{}\ must\ be\ before\ "{}a"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}desc"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ b:\ number,\ C:\ number,\ a:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ type\ annotations\ to\ be\ in\ descending\ order.\ "{}C"{}\ must\ be\ before\ "{}b"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}asc"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ c:\ number,\ C:\ number,\ b:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ type\ annotations\ to\ be\ in\ ascending\ order.\ "{}b"{}\ must\ be\ before\ "{}C"{}.}

The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ number,\ b:\ number,\ c:\ (boolean\ |\ number)\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ foo,\ C:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ 1:\ number,\ 2:\ boolean,\ 10:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}desc"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ c:\ number,\ b:\ number,\ a:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}desc"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ C:\ number,\ b:\ string,\ a:\ \{\}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}desc"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ 10:\ number,\ 2:\ number,\ 1:\ boolean\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ b:\ number,\ a:\ number\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a:\ string,\ b():\ number,\ c:\ boolean\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\ a():\ string,\ b:\ number,\ c:\ boolean\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-type-union-intersection-members}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-type-union-intersection-members}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10522}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$sort-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members$<$/code$>$}{<code>sort-type-union-intersection-members</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10522}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces that members of a type union/intersection are sorted alphabetically.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-type-union-intersection-members-options-16}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-sort-type-union-intersection-members-options-16}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10523}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10523}
You can specify the sort order using {\ttfamily order}.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}asc"{}} (default) -\/ enforce ascending sort order.
\item {\ttfamily "{}desc"{}} -\/ enforce descending sort order.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/sort-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}order"{}:\ "{}asc"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can disable checking intersection types using {\ttfamily check\+Intersections}.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true} (default) -\/ enforce sort order of intersection members.
\item {\ttfamily false} -\/ do not enforce sort order of intersection members.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/sort-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}checkIntersections"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can disable checking union types using {\ttfamily check\+Unions}.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily true} (default) -\/ enforce sort order of union members.
\item {\ttfamily false} -\/ do not enforce sort order of union members.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/sort-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}checkUnions"{}:\ true}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


You can specify the ordering of groups using {\ttfamily group\+Order}.

Each member of the type is placed into a group, and then the rule sorts alphabetically within each group. The ordering of groups is determined by this option.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily keyword} -\/ Keyword types ({\ttfamily any}, {\ttfamily string}, etc)
\item {\ttfamily named} -\/ Named types ({\ttfamily A}, `A\mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}prop'\mbox{]}{\ttfamily ,}B\mbox{[}\mbox{]}{\ttfamily ,}Array$<$\+C$>${\ttfamily ) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}literal{\ttfamily -\/ Literal types (}1{\ttfamily ,}\textquotesingle{}b\textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily ,}true{\ttfamily , etc) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}function{\ttfamily -\/ Function types (}() =\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} void{\ttfamily ) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}object{\ttfamily -\/ Object types (}\{ a\+: string \}{\ttfamily ,}\{ \mbox{[}key\+: string\mbox{]}\+: number \}{\ttfamily ) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}tuple{\ttfamily -\/ Tuple types (}\mbox{[}A, B, C\mbox{]}{\ttfamily ) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}intersection{\ttfamily -\/ Intersection types (}A \& B{\ttfamily ) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}union{\ttfamily -\/ Union types (}A \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|} B{\ttfamily ) \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}nullish{\ttfamily -\/}null{\ttfamily and}undefined\`{}
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/sort-\/type-\/union-\/intersection-\/members"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}groupOrder"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 'keyword',}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:

\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T1\ =\ B\ |\ A;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ union\ members\ to\ be\ in\ ascending\ order.\ "{}A"{}\ should\ be\ before\ "{}B"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T2\ =\ \{\ b:\ string\ \}\ \&\ \{\ a:\ string\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ intersection\ members\ to\ be\ in\ ascending\ order.\ "{}\{\ a:\ string\ \}"{}\ should\ be\ before\ "{}\{\ b:\ string\ \}"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ T3\ =\ [1,\ 2,\ 4]\ \&\ [1,\ 2,\ 3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Expected\ intersection\ members\ to\ be\ in\ ascending\ order.\ "{}[1,\ 2,\ 3]"{}\ should\ be\ before\ "{}[1,\ 2,\ 4]"{}.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
