 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10524}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$space-\/after-\/type-\/colon$<$/code$>$}{<code>space-after-type-colon</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10524}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent spacing after the type annotation colon.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-space-after-type-colon-options-17}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-space-after-type-colon-options-17}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10525}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10525}
This rule has a string argument.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}always"{}} (default)\+: Require a space after the type annotation colon (e.\+g. foo\+: Bar\+Type).
\item {\ttfamily "{}never"{}}\+: Require no spaces after the type annotation colon (e.\+g. foo\+:Bar\+Type).
\end{DoxyItemize}

This rule has an option object.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}allow\+Line\+Break"{}} -\/ Allow a line break to count as a space following the annotation colon.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}true"{}}\+: Enable
\item {\ttfamily "{}false"{}}\+: Disable
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\{ "{}rules"{}\+: \{ "{}flowtype/space-\/after-\/type-\/colon"{}\+: \mbox{[} 2, "{}always"{}, \{ "{}allow\+Line\+Break"{}\+: false \} \mbox{]} \} \}

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ \ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:(()\ =>\ void))\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ (()\ =>\ void))\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ \ (()\ =>\ void))\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{\ lorem,\ ipsum,\ dolor\ \}\ :\ \ \ SomeType)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ after\ "{}\{\ lorem,\ ipsum,\ dolor\ \}"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ number\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{\ a,\ b\ \}\ :\{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ number\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ "{}\{\ a,\ b\ \}"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{([\ a,\ b\ ]\ :string[])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ "{}[\ a,\ b\ ]"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(i?:number)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ "{}i"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(i?:\ \ number)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ after\ "{}i"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(i?:\ number)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ after\ "{}i"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ number\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ not\ be\ a\ line\ break\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ number\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ not\ be\ a\ line\ break\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{\{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ number\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ not\ be\ a\ line\ break\ after\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{():Object\ =>\ \{\}}

\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ barType:\ (string\ |\ ()\ =>\ void)\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ barType:\ ((string\ |\ ()\ =>\ void))\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ barType:(string\ |\ ()\ =>\ void)\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Foo\ =\ \{\ barType:((string\ |\ ()\ =>\ void))\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get():\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get<X>():\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get():\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get<X>():\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get:\ ()\ =>\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get:\ <X>()\ =>\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get:()\ =>\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ get:<X>()\ =>\ A;\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ +foo:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ +foo?:\ string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ +foo:string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ +foo?:string\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ [a:\ b]:\ c\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ [a:b]:c\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ +[a:\ b]:\ c\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ +[a:b]:c\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ [string]:\ c\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{\ [string]:c\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ x\ =\ (\{\}:\{\})}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ x\ =\ (\{\}:\ \{\})}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{((x):(string))}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{((x):\ (string))}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ x:\ number\ =\ 7;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{let\ x:\ number\ =\ 42;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ x:\ number\ =\ 42;}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-space-before-generic-bracket}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-space-before-generic-bracket}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10526}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$space-\/before-\/generic-\/bracket$<$/code$>$}{<code>space-before-generic-bracket</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10526}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent spacing before the opening {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}} of generic type annotation parameters.

This rule takes one argument. If it is `\textquotesingle{}never'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when there is a space before the}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}{\ttfamily . If it is}\textquotesingle{}always\textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when there is no space before the}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\`{}.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}never'\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise\ <string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation\ bracket}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise\ <string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation\ bracket}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise\ \ <string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation\ bracket}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation\ bracket}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise\ \ <string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ one\ space\ before\ "{}Promise"{}\ generic\ type\ annotation\ bracket}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise<string>}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ Promise\ <string>}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-space-before-type-colon}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-space-before-type-colon}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10527}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$space-\/before-\/type-\/colon$<$/code$>$}{<code>space-before-type-colon</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10527}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent spacing before the type annotation colon.

This rule takes one argument. If it is `\textquotesingle{}always'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when there is no space before the type annotation colon. If it is}\textquotesingle{}never\textquotesingle{}{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when there is a space before the type annotation colon. The default value is}\textquotesingle{}never\textquotesingle{}\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo\ :\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo\ ?\ :\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo\ \ :\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo?:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo\ ?\ \ :\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo\ \ ?:\ string)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{\ lorem,\ ipsum,\ dolor\ \}\ :\ SomeType)\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\{\ lorem,\ ipsum,\ dolor\ \}"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(foo\ :\ \{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ number\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{(\{\ a,\ b\ \}\ :\ \{\ a:\ string,\ b:\ number\ \})\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\{\ a,\ b\ \}"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{([\ a,\ b\ ]\ :\ string[])\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}[\ a,\ b\ ]"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{()\ :\ x\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ return\ type\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{():\ x\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ return\ type\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{()\ \ :\ x\ =>\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ before\ return\ type\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x(foo\ :\ string)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x(foo:\ string)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ x\ =\ function\ (foo\ :\ string)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ x\ =\ function\ (foo:\ string)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{class\ Foo\ \{\ constructor(foo\ :\ string\ )\ \{\}\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}

\DoxyCodeLine{async\ function\ foo(\{\ lorem,\ ipsum,\ dolor\ \}\ :\ SomeType)\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}\{\ lorem,\ ipsum,\ dolor\ \}"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ a()\ :\ x\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ return\ type\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ a():\ x\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ return\ type\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ a()\ \ :\ x\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ before\ return\ type\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (foo\ :string)\ =>\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (foo:string)\ =>\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (foo\ \ :string)\ =>\ string;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ 1\ space\ before\ "{}foo"{}\ parameter\ type\ annotation\ colon.}

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-spread-exact-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-spread-exact-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10528}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$spread-\/exact-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>spread-exact-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10528}
Enforce object types, that are spread to be exact type explicitly.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ bar\ =\ \{...\{test:\ string\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ \$Exact\ to\ make\ type\ spreading\ safe.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{test:\ number\};\ type\ bar\ =\ \{...foo\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Use\ \$Exact\ to\ make\ type\ spreading\ safe.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ bar\ =\ \{...\$Exact<\{test:\ string\}>\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{test:\ number\};\ type\ bar\ =\ \{...\$Exact<foo>\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-id-match}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-id-match}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10529}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$type-\/id-\/match$<$/code$>$}{<code>type-id-match</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10529}
Enforces a consistent naming pattern for type aliases.

\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-id-match-options-18}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-id-match-options-18}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10530}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10530}
This rule requires a text Reg\+Exp\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ "{}rules"{}:\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}flowtype/type-\/id-\/match"{}:\ [}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ 2,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ "{}\string^([A-\/Z][a-\/z0-\/9]*)+Type\$"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ]}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


`'\texorpdfstring{$^\wedge$}{\string^}(\mbox{[}A-\/Z\mbox{]}\mbox{[}a-\/z0-\/9\mbox{]}\texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*})+Type\$\$\textquotesingle{}\`{} is the default pattern.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{opaque\ type\ foo\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ identifier\ 'foo'\ does\ not\ match\ pattern\ '/\string^([A-\/Z][a-\/z0-\/9]*)+Type\$/u'.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ identifier\ 'foo'\ does\ not\ match\ pattern\ '/\string^([A-\/Z][a-\/z0-\/9]*)+Type\$/u'.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}\string^foo\$"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Type\ identifier\ 'FooType'\ does\ not\ match\ pattern\ '/\string^foo\$/u'.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ FooType\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}\string^foo\$"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ foo\ =\ \{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-import-style}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-import-style}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10531}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$type-\/import-\/style$<$/code$>$}{<code>type-import-style</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10531}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces a particular style for type imports\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ 'identifier'\ style}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{type\ T,\ type\ U,\ type\ V\}\ from\ '...';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ 'declaration'\ style}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ \{T,\ U,\ V\}\ from\ '...';}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-import-style-options-19}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-type-import-style-options-19}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10532}{}\doxyparagraph{\texorpdfstring{Options}{Options}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10532}
The rule has a string option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily "{}identifier"{}} (default)\+: Enforces that type imports are all in the \textquotesingle{}identifier\textquotesingle{} style.
\item {\ttfamily "{}declaration"{}}\+: Enforces that type imports are all in the \textquotesingle{}declaration\textquotesingle{} style.
\end{DoxyItemize}

This rule has an object option\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily ignore\+Type\+Default} -\/ if {\ttfamily true}, when in "{}identifier"{} mode, default type imports will be ignored. Default is {\ttfamily false}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ \{A,\ B\}\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ "{}import\ type"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}identifier"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ \{A,\ B\}\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ "{}import\ type"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}identifier"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ \{A,\ B\ as\ C\}\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ "{}import\ type"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}identifier"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ A\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ "{}import\ type"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}declaration"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{type\ A,\ type\ B\}\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ type\ import}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Unexpected\ type\ import}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{type\ A,\ type\ B\}\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}identifier"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ \{type\ A,\ type\ B\}\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}declaration"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ \{A,\ B\}\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}identifier"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ typeof\ *\ as\ A\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}identifier"{},\{"{}ignoreTypeDefault"{}:true\}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ A\ from\ 'a';}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}identifier"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ module\ "{}m"{}\ \{\ import\ type\ A\ from\ 'a';\ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-union-intersection-spacing}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-union-intersection-spacing}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10533}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$union-\/intersection-\/spacing$<$/code$>$}{<code>union-intersection-spacing</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10533}
{\itshape The {\ttfamily -\/-\/fix} option on the command line automatically fixes problems reported by this rule.}

Enforces consistent spacing around union and intersection type separators ({\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\vert$}{|}} and {\ttfamily \&}).

This rule takes one argument. If it is `\textquotesingle{}always'{\ttfamily then a problem is raised when there is no space around the separator. If it is}\textquotesingle{}never\textquotesingle{}\`{} then a problem is raised when there is a space around the separator.

The default value is `\textquotesingle{}always'\`{}.

The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string|\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string|\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ |number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string|number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{x:\ string\}|\{y:\ number\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ |\ number\ |boolean;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string|number|boolean;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (string)|\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ ((string))|(number\ |\ foo);}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ |number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string|\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ after\ union\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\&\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}always"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\&\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ \&number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ \{x:\ string\}\&\{y:\ number\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\&number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ \&\ number\ \&boolean;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\&number\&boolean;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (string)\&\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ ((string))\&(number\ \&\ foo);}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ a\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ \&number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ before\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\&\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ There\ must\ be\ no\ space\ after\ intersection\ type\ annotation\ separator}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ |\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ |\ number\ |\ boolean;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (string)\ |\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ ((string))\ |\ (number\ |\ foo);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string|number}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\ number}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x()\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\ number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string|\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ \&\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\ \&\ number\ \&\ boolean;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ (string)\ \&\ number;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ ((string))\ \&\ (number\ \&\ foo);}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Options:\ ["{}never"{}]}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\&number}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\&\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{\&\ number}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x()\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\&\ string}
\DoxyCodeLine{\&\ number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Settings:\ \{"{}flowtype"{}:\{"{}onlyFilesWithFlowAnnotation"{}:true\}\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ X\ =\ string\&\ number;}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-use-flow-type}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-use-flow-type}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10534}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$use-\/flow-\/type$<$/code$>$}{<code>use-flow-type</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10534}
Marks Flow \href{https://flowtype.org/docs/type-aliases.html}{\texttt{ type alias}} declarations as used.

Used to suppress \href{http://eslint.org/docs/rules/no-unused-vars}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily no-\/unused-\/vars}}} errors that are triggered by type aliases.

The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ class\ A\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/unused-\/vars"{}:1\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ function\ A():\ Y}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/unused-\/vars"{}:1\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ module\ A\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/unused-\/vars"{}:1\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ module\ A\ \{\ declare\ var\ a:\ Y\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/unused-\/vars"{}:1\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{declare\ var\ A:\ Y}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/unused-\/vars"{}:1\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ A\ from\ "{}a"{};\ type\ X<B\ =\ ComponentType<A>>\ =\ \{\ b:\ B\ \};\ let\ x:\ X;\ console.log(x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/unused-\/vars"{}:1\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{import\ type\ A\ from\ "{}a"{};\ type\ X<B\ =\ A<string>>\ =\ \{\ b:\ B\ \};\ let\ x:\ X;\ console.log(x);}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Additional\ rules:\ \{"{}no-\/unused-\/vars"{}:1\}}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-use-read-only-spread}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-use-read-only-spread}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10535}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$use-\/read-\/only-\/spread$<$/code$>$}{<code>use-read-only-spread</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10535}
Warns against accidentally creating an object which is no longer read-\/only because of how spread operator works in Flow. Imagine the following code\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ js}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +type:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +name:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


You might expect the identifier name to be read-\/only, however, that\textquotesingle{}s not true (\href{https://flow.org/try/\#0C4TwDgpgBAkgcgewCbQLxQN4B8BQUoDUokAXFAM7ABOAlgHYDmANDlgL4DcOOx0MKdYDQBmNCFSjpseKADp58ZBBb4CdAIYBbCGUq1GLdlxwBjBHUpQAHmX4RBIsRKlQN2sgHIPTKL08eoTm4rWV5JKA8AZQALBABXABskVwRgKAAjaAB3WmB1dISIAEIPLhC3NAiY+KSUtMyoHJo8guLSnCA}{\texttt{ flow.\+org/try}})\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ js}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ x:\ Identifier\ =\ \{\ name:\ '',\ type:\ ''\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{x.type\ =\ 'must\ NOT\ be\ writable!';\ //\ No\ Flow\ error}
\DoxyCodeLine{x.name\ =\ 'must\ NOT\ be\ writable!';\ //\ No\ Flow\ error}

\end{DoxyCode}


This rule suggests to use {\ttfamily \$Read\+Only\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} to prevent accidental loss of readonly-\/ness\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ js}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +name:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\}>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ x:\ Identifier\ =\ \{\ name:\ '',\ type:\ ''\ \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{x.type\ =\ 'must\ NOT\ be\ writable!';\ //\ \$FlowExpectedError[cannot-\/write]}
\DoxyCodeLine{x.name\ =\ 'must\ NOT\ be\ writable!';\ //\ \$FlowExpectedError[cannot-\/write]}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{||\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +aaa:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Flow\ type\ with\ spread\ property\ and\ all\ readonly\ properties\ must\ be\ wrapped\ in\ '\$ReadOnly<>'\ to\ prevent\ accidental\ loss\ of\ readonly-\/ness.}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{||\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +aaa:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +bbb:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{//\ Message:\ Flow\ type\ with\ spread\ property\ and\ all\ readonly\ properties\ must\ be\ wrapped\ in\ '\$ReadOnly<>'\ to\ prevent\ accidental\ loss\ of\ readonly-\/ness.}

\end{DoxyCode}


The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{||\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ name:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{||\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ name:\ string,\ //\ writable\ on\ purpose}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +surname:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +name:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{||\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ +name:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\}>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{||\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ name:\ string,\ //\ writable\ on\ purpose}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\}>;}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ INode\ =\ \{||\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{type\ Identifier\ =\ \$ReadOnly<\{|}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ ...INode,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ -\/name:\ string,}
\DoxyCodeLine{|\}>;}

\end{DoxyCode}


\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-valid-syntax}%
\Hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_eslint-plugin-flowtype-rules-valid-syntax}%
 \hypertarget{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10536}{}\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{$<$code$>$valid-\/syntax$<$/code$>$}{<code>valid-syntax</code>}}\label{md_node__modules_2eslint-plugin-flowtype_2README_autotoc_md10536}
{\bfseries{Deprecated}} Babylon (the Babel parser) v6.\+10.\+0 fixes parsing of the invalid syntax this plugin warned against.

Checks for simple Flow syntax errors.

The following patterns are not considered problems\+:


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x(foo:\ string\ =\ "{}1"{})\ \{\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{function\ x(foo:\ Type\ =\ bar())\ \{\}}

\end{DoxyCode}
